
The parity check matrix for the dual of W(3,23) minus a spread is a 23b x 
24b matrix, where b is 530.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the qx(q+1) rep matrix is given by \
Hrep.

The length of the code is 12720 and the check matrix has rank 
6625, so the full code has dimension 6095.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi cyclic 
11b x 13b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 5830 so the rate is 0.4583333333333333.
